<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sanctus.html>sanctus</a> (100221)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>Perfect</a> passive <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sanciō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">consecrate, <a href = vnd.unilang:appoint.html>appoint</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sacred.html>sacred</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle"><a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>Participle</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="la">sānctus</strong> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:feminine.html>feminine</a></i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">sāncta</b>, <i>neuter</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">sānctum</b>, <i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">sānctior</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">sānctissimus</b>); <i><a href = vnd.unilang:first.html>first</a>/second-declension <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></i>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:sacred.html>sacred</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:made.html>made</a> inviolable, having <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> established <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sacred.html>sacred</a>.</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sap.html>sap</a> (6089)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:sap.html>sap</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:sap.html>sap</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sapą</i>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sap.html>sap</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Saft</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:high.html>High</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a> <i>saf</i>).<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:high.html>High</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sadaz</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:savanne.html>savanne</a> (43112)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language"><a href = vnd.unilang:spanish.html>Spanish</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">sabana</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ta%C3%ADno_language" class="extiw" title="w:Taíno language">Taíno</a></span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:current.html>current</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> influenced <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">savane</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:savanne.html>savanne</a></i>.
